                    function populateul(urlval,divval){
						try{
    						var xmlhttp=false;
    						var status=0;
    						xmlhttp = window.XMLHttpRequest?new XMLHttpRequest():
    						new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
    						if (xmlhttp){
        						xmlhttp.onreadystatechange=function(){
            						if (xmlhttp.readyState==4){
                						if (xmlhttp.status==200){
                						    document.getElementById(divval).innerHTML=xmlhttp.responseText;
                						}
                						else if (xmlhttp.status==404) status=0
                						else status=0
        						    }
        						}
        						xmlhttp.open("GET",urlval,true);
        						xmlhttp.send(null);
						    }
					    }
						catch (e){xmlhttp = false;}
					}

                    function populateul(urlval,divval){
						try{
    						var xmlhttp=false;
    						var status=0;
    						xmlhttp = window.XMLHttpRequest?new XMLHttpRequest():
    						new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
    						if (xmlhttp){
        						xmlhttp.onreadystatechange=function(){
            						if (xmlhttp.readyState==4){
                						if (xmlhttp.status==200){
                						    document.getElementById(divval).innerHTML=xmlhttp.responseText;
                						}
                						else if (xmlhttp.status==404) status=0
                						else status=0
        						    }
        						}
        						xmlhttp.open("GET",urlval,true);
        						xmlhttp.send(null);
						    }
					    }
						catch (e){xmlhttp = false;}
					}

                    $(document).ready(function () {
                        if($('#itemContainer').is(':empty')){
    					    if(location.href.indexOf('toidev')>-1){console.log('No content received, initiating ajax call')}
    					    populateul('/latestsharedv3.cms?tag='+tagForAjax, 'itemContainer');
    					}

    					$('#ulItemContainer').show();
				        $('#ulItemContainer ul').attr('id', 'itemContainer');

				        if(typeof(tagForAjax) !== 'undefined' && ( (tagForAjax != "latestmostread") && (tagForAjax != "latestmostemail"))){
    				        $("div.holder").jPages({
                                containerID: "itemContainer",
                                perPage: 20,
                                keyBrowse: true,
                                scrollBrowse: false
                            });

                            $('.holder a').click(function() {
                                $('html, body').animate({
                                        scrollTop: $(".header_top").offset().top
                                }, 0);
                            });
				        }
                    });
                </script></div></div>

                    function populateul(urlval,divval){
						try{
    						var xmlhttp=false;
    						var status=0;
    						xmlhttp = window.XMLHttpRequest?new XMLHttpRequest():
    						new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
    						if (xmlhttp){
        						xmlhttp.onreadystatechange=function(){
            						if (xmlhttp.readyState==4){
                						if (xmlhttp.status==200){
                						    document.getElementById(divval).innerHTML=xmlhttp.responseText;
                						}
                						else if (xmlhttp.status==404) status=0
                						else status=0
        						    }
        						}
        						xmlhttp.open("GET",urlval,true);
        						xmlhttp.send(null);
						    }
					    }
						catch (e){xmlhttp = false;}
					}

                    $(document).ready(function () {
                        if($('#itemContainer').is(':empty')){
    					    if(location.href.indexOf('toidev')>-1){console.log('No content received, initiating ajax call')}
    					    populateul('/latestsharedv3.cms?tag='+tagForAjax, 'itemContainer');
    					}

    					$('#ulItemContainer').show();
				        $('#ulItemContainer ul').attr('id', 'itemContainer');

				        if(typeof(tagForAjax) !== 'undefined' && ( (tagForAjax != "latestmostread") && (tagForAjax != "latestmostemail"))){
    				        $("div.holder").jPages({
                                containerID: "itemContainer",
                                perPage: 20,
                                keyBrowse: true,
                                scrollBrowse: false
                            });

                            $('.holder a').click(function() {
                                $('html, body').animate({
                                        scrollTop: $(".header_top").offset().top
                                }, 0);
                            });
				        }
                    });
                </script></div>
